Almost every technology enthusiast👨🏻‍💻👩🏻‍💻 dreams to land a job in one of the FAANG companies.

Wondering what are FAANG companies?🤔
Don't worry, FAANG companies are:-

FACEBOOK - FACE😄 stored in a BOOK📘
AMAZON - AMAZing ON product
APPLE - APPs are LovE
NETFLIX - interNET used to FLIX
GOOGLE - GO Over GLobE🌏
Everyone aspires to be a part of one of these company but somewhere lacks on how to ace the race.🏁🏁🏁

As a christmas present, *GeeksForGeeks (GFG) student chapter along with CodeChef student chapter under the umbrella of ELIXIR Tech Fest 2021 ABESEC brings you a workshop covering on the roadmap to land yourself a job in FAANG companies.*

The workshop will be conducted by ABESEC alumni *Ms. Saloni Tyagi and ABESEC fourth year student Mr. Akash Garg who with their determination and hard work got placed in Amazon*. They will share with us their experience and will guide all the young coding enthusiasts🔥 the path to land themselves in FAANG companies. If they can then why we can't.

If you have a question in mind and feels like it is to be addressed during the session please fill this form : https://forms.gle/efHtfHAYSbD2x3mB6

So, do join this wonderful session on *19th of December 2020* at 4 p.m. Sharp.
The link for meeting would be shared on our discord server :https://discord.gg/yzsDjRbnyR
